[30;1m9 | [0m[35mOne way of handling imbalanced datasets is to reduce the number of observations from[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35mall classes but the minority class. The minority class is that with the least number[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35mof observations. The most well known algorithm in this group is random[0m
[30;1m12 | [0m[35mundersampling, where samples from the targeted classes are removed at random.[0m
[30;1m13 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m14 | [0m[35mBut there are many other algorithms to help us reduce the number of observations in the[0m
[30;1m15 | [0m[35mdataset. These algorithms can be grouped based on their undersampling strategy into:[0m

[31m--[ [0m[34mMatch #[0m[33m108[0m[34m of [0m[33m403[0m[31m ]--[0m
   Rule Id: [34mBD000610[0m

  Severity: [36mModerate[0m, Confidence: [36mLow[0m

[30;1m418 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m419 | [0m[35mIn an attempt to remove the noisy observations introduced by[0m
[30;1m420 | [0m[35m:class:`CondensedNearestNeighbour`, :class:`OneSidedSelection`[0m
[30;1m421 | [0m[35mwill first find the observations that are hard to classify, and then will use[0m

[30;1m423 | [0m[35m:class:`OneSidedSelection` runs as follows:[0m
[30;1m424 | [0m[35m[0m

[30;1m292 | [0m[35m:class:`EditedNearestNeighbours` carries out the following steps:[0m
[30;1m293 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m294 | [0m[35m1. Train a K-Nearest neighbours using the entire dataset.[0m
[30;1m295 | [0m[35m2. Find each observations' K closest neighbours (only for the targeted classes).[0m
[30;1m296 | [0m[35m3. Remove observations if any or most of its neighbours belong to a different class.[0m
[30;1m297 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m298 | [0m[35mBelow the code implementation::[0m

[30;1m167 | [0m[35mchallenge while at the same time becoming more and more common.[0m
[30;1m168 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m169 | [0m[35mOne way of addressing this issue is by re-sampling the dataset as to offset this[0m
[30;1m170 | [0m[35mimbalance with the hope of arriving at a more robust and fair decision boundary[0m
